					<p class="p-lg margin-top-0 margin-bottom-4">NISAR will help us track disasters, monitor ecosystems and crops, study glaciers and ice sheets, and understand how Earth’s surface moves and changes. The data it provides will help protect lives, support the management of natural resources, and give us a deeper understanding of our changing planet than ever before.</p>
					<div class="display-block tablet:display-flex desktop:display-flex flex-align-center">
						<div class="margin-right-3 margin-bottom-2 tablet:margin-bottom-0 desktop:margin-bottom-0">
							<ul class="social-icons social-icons-monochrome social-icons-round">
															</ul>
						</div>
											</div>
				</div>
				<div class="grid-col-12 desktop:grid-col-6 padding-left-0 desktop:padding-left-10">
					<div class="grid-row margin-bottom-4">
						<div class="grid-col-6">
							<div class="margin-bottom-1">
								<p class="label margin-0 color-carbon-50-important">Type</p>
							</div>
							<div class="p-lg font-weight-bold margin-0 padding-0 line-height-sm">Orbiter</div>
						</div>
						<div class="grid-col-6">
							<div class="margin-bottom-1">
								<p class="label margin-0 color-carbon-50-important">Launch</p>
							</div>
							<div class="p-lg font-weight-bold margin-0 padding-0 line-height-sm">July 30, 2025</div>
						</div>
					</div>
					<div class="grid-row">
						<div class="grid-col-6">
							<div class="margin-bottom-1">
								<p class="label margin-0 color-carbon-50-important">Partners</p>
							</div>
							<div class="p-lg font-weight-bold margin-0 padding-0 line-height-sm">NASA, Indian Space Research Organization (ISRO)</div>
						</div>
						<div class="grid-col-6">
							<div class="margin-bottom-1">
								<p class="label margin-0 color-carbon-50-important">Objective</p>
							</div>
							<div class="p-lg font-weight-bold margin-0 padding-0 line-height-sm">To measure and understand changes in Earth’s land, ice, water, and vegetation</div>
						</div>
					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
	</div>
		</div>




<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Mission Partners</strong><br>NASA,&nbsp;ISRO</li>



<li><strong>Instruments</strong><br>L-band SAR (24 cm wavelength) and S-band SAR (9.4 cm wavelength)</li>



<li><strong>Instrument Type</strong><br>Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR)</li>



<li><strong>Mission Phase</strong><br>Commissioning phase</li>



<li><strong>Data Availability</strong><br>NISAR data is being archived by<a href="https://www.earthdata.nasa.gov/centers/asf-daac"> the Alaska Satellite Facility (ASF) DAAC</a> and is openly available to the public. A small collection of sample data generated from NISAR acquisitions <a href="https://www.earthdata.nasa.gov/news/nisar-sample-data-products-available">is already available to explore,</a> with more to come soon.</li>
</ul>

				<div class="margin-bottom-10 display-none tablet:display-block desktop:display-block">
					<h3 class="label"></h3>
					<h2 class="display-41 margin-0">Mission Overview</h2>
				</div>
				<p class="heading-22 margin-bottom-2">An Unprecedented View of Earth</p>
				<p class="p-md">NISAR's data can help people worldwide better manage natural resources and hazards, as well as providing information for scientists to better understand the effects and pace of climate change. It will also add to our understanding of our planet's hard outer layer, called its crust.</p>

		<div class="grid-row flex-align-center">
			<div class="grid-col-12 desktop:grid-col-6 padding-x-3 desktop:padding-right-5 margin-bottom-5">
				<div class="label margin-bottom-2"></div>
				<h2 class="page-heading-md">The Magic of SAR</h2>
				<p class="p-md">NISAR will be the first radar of its kind in space to systematically map Earth, using two different radar frequencies (L-band and S-band) to measure changes of our planet’s surface, including movements as small as centimeter. Synthetic aperture radar (SAR) refers to a technique for producing fine-resolution images from a resolution-limited radar system.</p>
									<a href="https://science.nasa.gov/mission/nisar/get-to-know-sar/" target="_self" class="button-primary button-primary-md link-external-false" aria-label="">
						<span class="line-height-alt-1">Get to Know SAR</span>
						<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><circle class="button-primary-circle" cx="16" cy="16" r="16"></circle><path d="M8 16.956h12.604l-3.844 4.106 1.252 1.338L24 16l-5.988-6.4-1.252 1.338 3.844 4.106H8v1.912z" class="color-spacesuit-white"></path></svg>
					</a>
					
			</div>
			<div class="grid-col-12 desktop:grid-col-6 desktop:padding-left-5">
				<div class="width-full">
					<div class="hds-media-wrapper margin-left-auto margin-right-auto"><figure class="hds-media-inner hds-cover-wrapper hds-media-ratio-cover "><video class="hds-video-background " alt="NISAR Imaging Animation" style="transform: scale(1); transform-origin: 50% 50%; object-position: 50% 50%; object-fit: cover;" autoplay="true" loop muted="true" playsinline="true"><source src="https://assets.science.nasa.gov/content/dam/science/missions/nisar/nisar-jpl/multimedia/3_PAR_SARImaging.mp4" type="video/mp4" /></video></figure></div>				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
	</div>

<script>
gform.initializeOnLoaded( function() {jQuery(document).trigger("gform_pre_post_render", [{ formId: "45", currentPage: "1", abort: function() { this.preventDefault(); } }]);        if (event && event.defaultPrevented) {                return;        }        const gformWrapperDiv = document.getElementById( "gform_wrapper_45" );        if ( gformWrapperDiv ) {            const visibilitySpan = document.createElement( "span" );            visibilitySpan.id = "gform_visibility_test_45";            gformWrapperDiv.insertAdjacentElement( "afterend", visibilitySpan );        }        const visibilityTestDiv = document.getElementById( "gform_visibility_test_45" );        let postRenderFired = false;        function triggerPostRender() {            if ( postRenderFired ) {                return;            }            postRenderFired = true;            gform.core.triggerPostRenderEvents( 45, 1 );            if ( visibilityTestDiv ) {                visibilityTestDiv.parentNode.removeChild( visibilityTestDiv );            }        }        function debounce( func, wait, immediate ) {            var timeout;            return function() {                var context = this, args = arguments;                var later = function() {                    timeout = null;                    if ( !immediate ) func.apply( context, args );                };                var callNow = immediate && !timeout;                clearTimeout( timeout );                timeout = setTimeout( later, wait );                if ( callNow ) func.apply( context, args );            };        }        const debouncedTriggerPostRender = debounce( function() {            triggerPostRender();        }, 200 );        if ( visibilityTestDiv && visibilityTestDiv.offsetParent === null ) {            const observer = new MutationObserver( ( mutations ) => {                mutations.forEach( ( mutation ) => {                    if ( mutation.type === 'attributes' && visibilityTestDiv.offsetParent !== null ) {                        debouncedTriggerPostRender();                        observer.disconnect();                    }                });            });            observer.observe( document.body, {                attributes: true,                childList: false,                subtree: true,                attributeFilter: [ 'style', 'class' ],            });        } else {            triggerPostRender();        }    } );
</script>
